in front of Sora, who grits his teeth and takes it down in one strike. The 
fist returns to Baymax's arm and he lands near them)

Sora: Nice, Baymax!

(Baymax raises a fist)

Sora: What?

Baymax: Now, we fist bump.

Sora: Fist bump?

Baymax: To display excitement. Hiro taught it to me.

Sora: So, like...this?

(Sora taps his fist against Baymax's, while Donald does the same with Goofy's)

Baymax: Bah-la-la-la-la-la-la.

(Baymax flutters his fingers upward in the air)

Sora: Bah-la-la-la-la-la-la?

(Sora, Donald, and Goofy do the same with confused looks. Suddenly, a Metal 
Troll drops from the building behind them. The three summons their weapons)

Goofy: Get ready!

(They rush forward)

Sora: Another one?!

Honey Lemon: We're here!

(They turn to see Hiro, Fred, Wasabi, and Honey Lemon ready to fight)

Wasabi: Ugh! Can't we pick on one our own size?

(Go Go rolls in)

Go Go: It looks the right size to me.

Fred: Watch me scorch 'em with my freeze-nado! The only tornado made of

Sora: Prepare to face Keyblade Hero 3!

Hiro: And the crime fighting team of Big Hero 6! Together, we're unstoppable.

(They run forward and clash with the Metal Troll. Later, the group relaxes

Fred: Was that awesome...or was that TOTALLY AWESOME?! Haha! Jumping!

Goofy: You just made Donald's day.

(Honey Lemon giggles. They sit and watch the sunset)

Hiro: My brother wanted to help people. Now, we try to do the same.

Sora: Your brother?

Hiro (looking down): Yeah, Tadashi. There was a fire, and now he's gone.

(Go Go shares Hiro's grief)

Hiro: But he always wanted to make a difference. He cared about people. 
That's why he worked so hard to create Baymax.

Sora: I'm sorry.

(Hiro and Sora take bites of their ice cream)

Hiro: He's still here. In Baymax. In all of us.

Sora: Tadashi--he lives on in your hearts.

Hiro: Yeah. Right. He will always be a part of us in some way.

(Sora leans back)

Sora: And when you're not strong enough, he'll make up the difference.

(Morning bells ring and Sora becomes Roxas as Hayner, Pence and Olette eat 
sea-salt ice cream beside him, if only for a moment)

Hiro: Sora. You okay?

Sora: Yeah. Fine.

(Hiro takes another bite as Sora looks down at his hand, coming to his 
senses, and places it over his heart)

Sora: I'm with you.

(Later at night, the friends walk through the city together. Fred stretches 
after a long day while Hiro and Sora chat. They hear an odd sound woosh 
behind them and whirl around)

Sora: What?!

Goofy: What's that?

(They see a jellyfish-shaped cluster of blocks floating through the air)

Go Go: Great, they're back.

Wasabi: Oh, we got this.

Honey Lemon: Time for a lesson.

(Fred closes his hood and jumps ahead)

Fred: Cheee-aaarge!

(Fred, Wasabi, Honey Lemon and Go Go charge ahead after the strange entity.

Hiro: Wait! Uh, guys! That one's not like the others!

(They fail to hear him)

Hiro: It can't be. Microbots?

Sora: Microbots? You know what they are?

Goofy: Well, they're different from Heartless.

Donald: Uh-huh.

Hiro: Microbots are designed to do whatever you think via a neural

(He trails off upon seeing their ever-more confused faces)

Hiro: They're kind of a mini-bot I invented. Some bad stuff happened and

(He gasps)

Hiro: Could it be?

Hiro: I'm gonna go back to the garage and look into it some more. You mind

Donald: You bet!

Goofy: Of course!

Sora: We need you on the sciency stuff.

Baymax: Sora, Donald, Goofy, I will be your personal healthcare companion.

Hiro: Sora, I just marked the target's position. Look for the indicator.

Baymax: Target acquired.

Hiro: They're not microbots... Be careful!

Sora: It's no fair! Why can't we hurt it?

Goofy: What do we do?

Sora: This is weird.

Wasabi: Now he tells us.

Hiro: Team, check in.

Honey Lemon: No, Hiro!

(Honey Lemon pops out a yellow chem-ball from her purse as the Darkubes

Honey Lemon: We'll gather as much data from the Darkubes as we can.

Wasabi: Hiro, figure out a way for us to beat this thing!

(He looks up and jumps just in time to dodge another strike. Go Go blades

(He nods)

Hiro: Fine. I'll look for a way that we can expose the Darkubes' core. Just

Everyone: Copy.

Sora: Hiro, what should WE do?

(Hiro busily types away at his computer)

Hiro: You protect the others.

(A map appears on the screen with the locations of the four heroes)

Hiro: I'll mark their position for you on your AR display.

Sora, Donald & Goofy: We got it!

(They summon their weapons)

Sora: Time to go, Baymax!

Baymax: All right.

Hiro: Sora, the Darkubes are gonna be tricky to bust open. You'll have to

Sora: Improvise! I know.

Hiro: Cool. Good luck!

(In the Central District they reach Honey Lemon's indicator, but don't see 
her)

Sora: Honey Lemon!

Honey Lemon: Hey, Sora? I think I'm stuck. See if you can find the residue 
from my chem-balls. If you hit it with fire or electricity, it might trigger 
a chain reaction!

(The Darkubes holding Honey Lemon are gathered in the center, with each arm

Honey Lemon: Gracias, Sora! Next time I won't go so easy on them.

(She hops away)

Hiro: Honey Lemon! I'm glad you're safe.

(They approach Wasabi's indicator at the top of a blue-ringed skyscraper 
where he finds a large orb of Darkubes)

Sora: Wasabi! Can you hear me?

Wasabi: Sora! Am I glad to see you! I am not a big fan of heights. Hey, you 
think it dragged me up here 'cause it's scared of being attacked from

(Sora leaps over a high-powered fan, which sends him soaring over the 
Darkubes. On his descent, he readies his Keyblade with a laugh, slamming

Wasabi: Finally! Thanks for the save, Sora. I'll see if anyone else needs 
help.

(He jumps to the edge of the building and, swallowing his fear, leaps off)

Hiro: Wasabi, good to see you're all right.

(Sora descends the building, seeing a large rolling ball made of Darkubes 
which matches Go Go's indicator)

Sora: Go Go! Are you in there?

Go Go: Sora! I don't know how to stop this thing. I tried slowing it down 
with my discs.

Goofy: You see anything big you can smash against it?

Donald: Hey... What about that big red thing from the shugyo?

(They pass the giant red ball from earlier and Sora leaps aboard)

Go Go: Sora! C'mon, hurry!

(Sora rides the ball through the North District to cut off the rolling 
Darkube in its path. He crashes it directly into the Darkubes, which

Go Go: Thanks. I owe ya.

Hiro: Doesn't look like you're hurt, Go Go.

(They reach Fred's indicator, where he is trapped in a bunch of Darkubes

Sora: Fred! You okay?

Fred: I'm getting pulled in too many directions! Do you think you can 
free my arms and legs? Gotta find a weak point and loosen the Darkubes' grip!

(Spinning horizontally on each light pole, the Darkubes' arms fall away 
and the central mass starts to give)

Fred: Yeah!

(The blocks explode in all directions as Fred leaps out of it)

Fred: Super juuump!

(He lands, making sure his hood stays on)

Fred: Pure appreciation, my man.

(He turns)

Fred: My citizens! They need me!

(He hops away)

Hiro: Glad you're okay, Fred. Listen, Sora! The Darkubes have converged 
on a single location.

(The Darkubes gather on the top of the tallest building in San Fransokyo)

Hiro: Whatever's happening can't be good. I'm almost done pinpointing the 
core. If you need me to help--

Sora: Nah, it's okay, Hiro. We're on it.

Hiro: Thanks.

Donald: Get a move on!

(The Darkubes resemble fireflies as they float in the air of the South 
District as Sora and company reach the top of the skyscraper. They amass 
into the largest orb of blocks so far, its outer layer rippling as they 
arrive)

Go Go: Okay, there's a lot of them.

Goofy: What do ya suppose they'll do?

Wasabi: I don't think we wanna find out.

(Fred hops closer)

Fred: I say we destroy this thing!

Donald: Yeah!

Honey Lemon: But without a strategy, we'd just be wasting our strength.

Sora: If we knew where to strike...

Hiro: Sora! I got it! I'm sending you an AR software update. It'll show you 
where the core is--the Darkubes' weak point. I'm coming to help.

(The AR display glitches like an old videotape)

Sora: Huh? That's weird. Is it busted?

(He attempts to press the button on his headset, but it has no effect. 
Looking ahead, he sees a cloaked figure walking in his direction)

Sora: Hiro, who's that on the display?

Goofy: That's not the display. He's really here.

Sora: Huh?

Go Go: The black coat... He's back?

????: Are you done messing around?

Sora: What? Wait, that voice...

Wasabi: Hold on. You...know this guy?

Fred: And now...enter the supervillain.

Honey Lemon: He definitely has the vibe.

(The figure removes his hood, revealing shoulder-length silver hair just 
like...)

Riku: Funny.

(Sora dispels his Keyblade)

Sora: Riku... But...

(Riku conjures a red object from thin air)

Riku: As if this stupid experiment wasn't already a hassle.

Hiro: Huh? Where'd he get that?

Sora: Hiro, do you recognize it?

Hiro: Yeah...

(Riku holds it up, peering at it with his yellow eyes)

Riku: Not quite ready.

Hiro: That's the first chip I made for Baymax. It's full of combat programs.

(The chip has a skull and crossbones drawn on it. Big Hero 6 reacts with 
shock and disbelief)

Sora: Programs?

Hiro: Yeah, they tell Baymax how to react.

Goofy: Does that mean...it's like his heart?

Donald: Kind of...

(Riku faces the Darkubes)

Riku: More then!

(He tosses the chip into the nest of Darkubes before vanishing in a corridor 
of darkness)

Sora: Riku!

(The Darkubes assume a heart shape and begin to spin uncontrollably, glowing 
a bright greenish-blue. Its arms lash out, knocking Go Go, Wasabi, Honey 
Lemon and Fred off the building)

Sora: Oh no!

Hiro: Sora, I'm on my way. I'll look after my team. You guys fight the 
Darkubes! Remember to use the AR device to target the core!

Sora: I got it!

(The Darkubes aim and shoot a spurt of blocks in their direction, but they

high for Sora to reach. Without warning the Darkubes glow red and slam 
into the ground, swiping away at the group before reassembling in the air 
as a giant fist. Sora dodges away as it narrowly misses a deadly punch 
from the blocky foe. Forming a heart shape again, Sora takes the initiative)

Sora: Baymax! Full thrust!

(Sora rides on Baymax's back)

Sora: Go, Baymax!

Baymax: Full speed!

(Baymax engages his rocket boots and flies through the center of the 
Darkubes. Sora and Baymax strike at the central core repeatedly until 
the outer blocks fall still, disappearing until only the central core 
is left. It falls to the ground and Sora releases a final strike, 
freeing the heart inside from the Heartless. The red chip clatters to 
the floor)

Hiro: Baymax...

(Hiro runs over and kneels to pick up the chip)

Riku: Oh, this isn't for you.

(Riku snatches it up first)

Riku: At least not until we're done.

(Hiro attempts to get it back, but Riku jumps to the top of a device on 
the roof)

Sora: Riku... Is it you? Why do you look like that?

Riku: Looks are deceiving, but the heart? You know that it's me.

Sora: I know Riku wouldn't do this. Not without a good reason.

Riku: A reason? When did that ever matter? We've been trying to one-up 
each other since we were kids.

Sora: What...?

(Donald and Goofy rush in front of Sora)

Donald: Don't listen to him, Sora!

Goofy: The coat means he's with Organization XIII! And THAT means he's 
not really Riku.

Dark Riku: Smarter than you look.

Goofy: We defeated Ansem and Xehanort--every last one of 'em. But still 
they all came back anyway, right? So, maybe this Riku "came back" too, 
from the time when Ansem possessed him.

Donald: Yeah, from the past!

Sora: What? How?

Dark Riku: Unlike a certain wizard you know, I had to play by the rules 
to travel through time. Which meant leaving my body behind.

(Sora remembers Young Xehanort's explanation of time travel)

Sora: I know about this...

(He looks up at Riku)

Sora: But...YOU HAVE a body.

(Riku smirks)

Dark Riku: Xehanort's heart left his body in order to voyage back through 
time. He needed to tell his younger self of the great plans he had in 
store. There in the past, his heart stayed, and waited out the years until 
you and I came along. Xehanort's heart possessed me and became Ansem, the 
first adversary you faced. The rest of him, the piece he left behind, took 
the name Xemnas and created the first Organization. It was all a part of a 
larger plan to bring Xehanort into contact with the right hearts--enough 
of them to form the real Organization XIII. They could come from anywhere, 
any WHEN...just as long as he had the right vessels at hand to place their 
hearts in.

Sora: Vessels?

Donald & Goofy: Replicas!

Dark Riku: That's right. The Replica Program was a success. We are as real 
as people.

(Sora dispels his Keyblade)

Sora: Then pack up and leave! What are you still doing here?

Dark Riku: To see if we can recreate a heart from data.

Sora: What?

Dark Riku (chuckling darkly): Sorry, did we steal your idea? That walking 
balloon over there has a "heart."

(He looks at the chip in his hand)

Dark Riku: At least that's the nonsense I'm supposed to believe.

Sora: There are hearts all around us. You only have to see them for them 
to become real.

Hiro: Where'd you get that? That's my chip. I made it.

Dark Riku: Oh, well, I'm sorry about that. But I promise I'll put it right 
back where I found it.

Hiro: What do you mean?

(Riku turns away from them)

Dark Riku: I think I'll be getting back to work now.

Sora: No!

Hiro: Wait!

(Riku vanishes)

Hiro: We gotta stop him. Guys--

(Hiro looks back to his friends, who are worn out from tonight's events)

Baymax: You are all suffering from acute exhaustion. I recommend rest.

Hiro: Yeah, you're right. Let's regroup.

(They return to Hiro's Garage)

Fred: C'mon, guys. What's with all the long faces?

(Fred jumps to the center of the room)

Fred: Did you forget that we WON?!

Go Go: Fred. Not now.

(He agrees and stops)

Hiro: His name is Riku? And you know him?

Sora: Yeah... Well, I know A "him."

Donald: That one is a fake!

Goofy: The fake one's with Organization XIII, our arch-nemenies.

Wasabi: Okay, but how'd he get Hiro's chip?

Honey Lemon: And what did he mean about an experiment?

Go Go: And what do they want?

Sora: He said they're trying to recreate a heart from data, but I don't 
know what they REALLY want. None of us do. These guys, they show up--and 
instead of fighting fair and square, they go for the heart and say things 
to try and get under your skin. They're cowards. And now, they're doing it 
to you, too. It's our fault.

(The trio look down)

Hiro: No. This could be good. That chip might finally be able to give me 
some answers.

Sora: You said that you made it, right?

Hiro: Yeah. This Baymax--he's actually the second model. Uh, no offense.

Baymax: I am a robot. I cannot be offended.

(Hiro smiles)

Hiro: It's a long story. But the first Baymax and the chip I made...vanished 
into another dimension along with the microbots. The chip's back... So the 
first Baymax might be back too.

Honey Lemon: Hiro...

(There is silence for a moment)

Baymax: Those who suffer a loss require support from friends and loved ones.

(He motions toward the others in the room and there is a big crash that 
shakes the entire building)

Fred: What was that?

Wasabi: I don't know.

(Hiro rushes to his computer and pulls up a breaking news broadcast reading 
"Mysterious Monsters Renew Attacks. Giant flying creature terrorizing San 
Fransokyo. Police to impose curfew." The screen shows a visual of the 
Darkubes)

Sora: Guys, c'mon!

Hiro: Team, let's go!

(Meanwhile, Maleficent and Pete walk along the overpass of the quiet city. 
Dark Riku enters behind them, causing them to turn around)

Dark Riku: Why are you snooping around?

Maleficent: That would be none of your concern.

Dark Riku: Overstep, and darkness will consume you again.

Maleficent: What an interesting thing to say. I shall do anything I please. 
As should you.

Dark Riku: Oh, I intend to.

(He leaves them)

Pete: Who's he? Friend of yours?

Maleficent: Yes. Though I could not tell you from "when."

(Later after sunrise, the gang finds the Darkubes above a tall building)

Go Go: Hope it's learned some new tricks.

Wasabi: Yeah, now it's gotta face ALL of us.

(Baymax lands on the roof)

Honey Lemon: That's right.

Fred: Freddie want to destroy!

Baymax: Our probability of success is--

Hiro: You don't have to crunch the numbers, Baymax.

(Hiro walks forward)

Hiro: It's not the sum of our parts. It's the sum of our hearts.

Sora: Yeah.

(Riku smiles)

Dark Riku: Which adds up to what?

(They look up to the flying wind sock, where Riku is perched, staring down 
at them)

Dark Riku: Show me.

(He leaps down off the wind sock, summoning the Soul Eater, using it to 
slice through the Darkubes core. He lands on the ground, dispelling his 
weapon as the Darkubes disintegrate. He stands, a piercing grin on his 
face, and holds up the chip, which brims with darkness)

Dark Riku: Almost there.

Sora: What?!

(Riku kicks a few of the blocks, which move slightly, glowing a faint red)

Dark Riku: This pile of junk collected the data we needed... The terror of 
being attacked without warning... The despair of having no place to run... 
The longing for vengeance...

Sora: A heart's more than that!

Wasabi: It's working together.

Donald & Goofy: Smiling at something funny.

Hiro: Trusting friends.

Sora: In every heart, there's hope.

Big Hero 6: Yeah!

Dark Riku: You're right.

Sora: Huh...?

Dark Riku: That's why I made sure our creation fought YOU. Now the data 
contains a complete heart.

Sora: A heart made from conflict? That can't be real.

Dark Riku (interrupting): What was it you said? I only have to see it for 
it to become real? So, let's see it.

(Riku turns toward the Darkubes and raises his arm. A dark portal appears 
in the sky and the Darkubes begin to float, being pulled as if by magnets 
into the portal, some glowing red, and others, green)

Dark Riku: First, we need a vessel.

(Once the Darkubes have all been gathered into the portal, they return out 
in a single round mass, all glowing red with lightning bolts dancing around 
its outside. It descends slowly, pulsating)

Go Go: What's going on?

Honey Lemon: Another Darkube form?

Fred: Doesn't look as bad as the last one.

(He chuckles nervously)

Goofy: It could be a trick.

Wasabi: Usually is.

Donald: We can stop it!

(The Darkubes begin to recede and a white arm emerges from the mass of 
blocks, surprising Hiro. Sora summons his Keyblade)

Sora: Yeah.

Hiro: Wait! That's...Baymax.

Sora: What?!

(Sora looks from Hiro to the Darkubes)

Sora: No way.

(They slowly recede from Baymax's body, but unlike his usual red armor, he 
is clad in a deep purple suit with spiked pauldrons. His right arm is 
covered in miniature Darkubes shaped in an oversized fist. He lands in 
front of Riku. Big Hero 6 exchange looks of concern)

Hiro: Baymax...

Dark Riku: Don't bother. This puppet has lost his heart. He won't wake up.

Hiro: He's not a puppet! Baymax, he's like my family. Please! Give me back 
my friend.

(Riku laughs darkly)

Dark Riku: Yes... I did promise I'd put this back where I found it.

(He lifts up the red chip and Dark Baymax's port opens as Riku inserts the 
chip. The port closes and Dark Baymax's eyes glow red)

Dark Riku: But there's one piece missing. Sora, you're the one who's going 
to complete this heart.

Sora: Yeah, right.

Dark Riku: You can't have a heart without sadness...without loss. You see, 
you're going to destroy Hiro's friend right in front of him.

(Riku disappears in a corridor of darkness)

Sora: Wait!

(Dark Baymax engages his wings and takes off into the sky. They realize that 
he's heading for Hiro)

Everyone: Hiro!

Baymax: Oh no.

(Go Go, Wasabi, Honey Lemon, and Fred try to intervene but Dark Baymax 
swipes them away. Sora, Donald and Goofy hold Dark Baymax back from Hiro, 
when Baymax 2.0 punches him away. Dark Baymax sails through the air and 
over the edge of the building. The others run back to Hiro)

Go Go, Wasabi, Honey Lemon & Fred: Hiro...

(Dark Baymax rises back to the roof, his Darkube arm becoming more of a 
claw. Donald and Goofy run forward)

Sora: Hiro, tell us. What should we do?

(Hiro clenches his fist)

Hiro: Baymax means everything to me. But that chip isn't who he is.

(Donald and Goofy hold Dark Baymax back)

Hiro: I already made this mistake once before. Tadashi wouldn't want there 
to be a Baymax that hurts people. Sora, he has to be stopped.

Sora: Okay. Help Go Go and the others. You can leave this guy to us.

Hiro: Thank you.

(Sora smiles before rushing forward just as Dark Baymax knocks Donald and 
Goofy away. He flies back up into the air)

Sora: Oh no!

Hiro: Sora, take Baymax!

Sora: Okay! Baymax!

Baymax: I am ready, Sora.

(Baymax readies his wings and flies to Sora, extending his arm. Sora grabs 
it and leaps on Baymax's back. They ascend into the skies of San Fransokyo, 
following Dark Baymax. They fly through the city streets as Dark Baymax 
shoots Darkubes back at them. Sora shoots magic bolts at Dark Baymax as 
Baymax 2.0 punches the Darkubes back at him. They sail through each 
District, over and under the railways in an effort to catch up with the 
dark robot. Dark Baymax pulses with purple energy as they corner him in 
the South District)

Sora: What?

(A surge flows through Dark Baymax and the red behind his eyes flash, 
Darkubes sparkling in the air around him. He strikes aggressively with his 
large claw and Baymax and Sora dodge backwards. Dark Baymax extends his 
wings and raises his arm, summoning a torrent of dark rain upwards that 
falls back down, cascading in Sora's direction. With a quick boost from 
Baymax's rocket boots, they aerial dodge as it narrowly misses them)

Sora: We'll stop him together!

Baymax: Understood.

(Baymax 2.0 flies at the Dark Baymax, performing an uppercut and 
interrupting his summoning of Darkubes. Immediately, Sora continues his 
barrage of magical bolts as Baymax pummels Dark Baymax)

Baymax: Knife Hand. Roundhouse. Hammer Fist.

(Sora leaps off of Baymax from above his dark doppelgänger and as Baymax 
persues Dark Baymax from behind, Sora drops in above him, knocking him 
away. Baymax swoops by and Sora grabs his extended hand, leaping onto his 
back again and dispelling his Keyblade. Baymax jolts, being pulled backwards 
as Dark Baymax grabs onto his rocket boots and swings Baymax and Sora 
toward the ground. Baymax regains his orientation and clutches Dark 
Baymax's own rocket boots, pulling him down. Sora screams as their descent 
results in a tussle through the air. Dark Baymax's large claw grasps 
Baymax's arm, but Baymax knocks it away and engages the rocket in his 
fist, punching Dark Baymax away from him. As Baymax reaches the ground, 
he slows his descent with his rocket boots as Dark Baymax crashes to the 
earth. Baymax 2.0 turns back as his fist returns to his suit. Sora leaps 
off Baymax and rushes to the dark robot, which sparks as electricity 
courses around the broken armor. Donald and Goofy arrive with the others)

Sora: Guys... Hiro...

(They rush past him and Hiro stops at the sight of the fallen Baymax)

Wasabi: So...did we stop him?

Hiro: Safety mode kicks in if he's put under too much stress, so he's 
probably just in stasis.

(He kneels down by his friend)

Hiro: We'll have to destroy the chip if we want to be certain.

Honey Lemon: But...are you sure?

Fred: Yeah, dude...you don't need to go THAT FAR.

Go Go: Maybe we can find another way.

(Hiro shakes his head and taps open the port on Dark Baymax's chest. He 
removes the red chip)

Hiro: It's the right thing to do.

(The Darkubes fly into the air in spirals as Baymax's armor starts to 
glow a bright red. The cubes blink away, leaving behind the white pillowy 
form of Baymax. Hiro places a hand on his friend)

Hiro: Tadashi would've done the same thing.

Sora: But Hiro...isn't that Baymax's heart?

(Hiro places a hand over his own heart)

Hiro: It's okay. Baymax is HERE.

(He opens his palm, looking down at the red chip)

Hiro: I...should be the one.

(Hiro destroys the chip. Later, they gather in Hiro's Garage)

Hiro: Ow?

(Eyes open)

Baymax: Hello, I am Baymax, your personal healthcare companion.

(They rejoice as Baymax is restored and Hiro rushes to hug him)

Fred: Two Baymaxes!

(Baymax 2.0 hugs Hiro as well as Goofy and Donald laugh, everyone chattering 
excitedly)

Sora: This is great, Hiro!

Hiro: Yeah, thanks.

Sora: So, uh, do you think I could take one of them with me?

Hiro: Uh, that's a no.

Sora: What? Come on.

Hiro: No. Who's gonna repair him?

Sora: One. Just one of them!

(Hiro sighs)

Sora: C'mon. Pleeease?

Hiro: He's MY personal healthcare companion?

(After unsuccessfully convincing Hiro, the three pals leave their new 
friends in the big city of San Fransokyo. They return to Le Grand Bistrot 
in Twilight Town. After giving Little Chef more ingredients, they walk out 
of the restaurant with Scrooge)

Sora: Hey, Little Chef, your bistro turned out to be a big hit! 

(The rat smiles and nods from atop Sora's head)

Goofy: Yeah, everybody in the whole town loves it.

Donald: Good idea, Uncle Scrooge.

Scrooge: Aye, naturally! But to be perfectly honest, I'm actually a wee 
bit surprised myself.

(He scratches his temple)

Goofy: Gawrsh, Uncle Scrooge, I thought you had this all planned out in 
advance.

(Sora turns to face Scrooge)

Sora: Wait, didn't you?

Scrooge: Oh, I had the business side of it planned down to the finest 
detail--the open air theatre, the flyers, the promo data--the whole kit 
and caboodle. But that wasn't enough. It was Little Chef's commitment to 
his craft--his desire to put smiles on everyone's faces--that made the 
bistro a success. A heart that cares that much is like a giant magnet that 
grabs ya and pulls ya right in.

Goofy: That must be why we like hangin' around Sora. Don'tcha think so, 
Donald?

Donald: Yeah!

Scrooge: Aye, and perhaps why Little Chef took such a shinin' to you in the 
first place.

(Sora's eyes move upward to Little Chef's direction. He moves his arm and 
the rat runs down to his hand, facing Sora. Sora chuckles and high-fives 
Little Chef with his finger)

Scrooge: Folks are hungry for connection, so you lads keep 'em well fed.

Sora: Sure thing! Right, Little Chef?

(Little Chef nods confidently, winking. Later, they return to their Gummi 
Ship. Sora's Gummiphone starts to ring and Jiminy leaps into his shoulder 
as he pulls it out)

Jiminy: Sora, somebody's callin' us on the Gummiphone.

(Donald and Goofy walk to Sora's chair and Sora answers the call. Dale 
appears on the screen way too close to the camera)

Dale: We got baaad news.

Sora: Huh?

(Chip yanks Dale away from the camera)

Chip: We totally lost contact with the King and Riku! They're all on their 
own in the realm of darkness!

Sora, Donald, Goofy & Jiminy: Whaaat?!

Sora: See? I knew I shoulda gone!

Donald: Chip, how do we get to 'em?

Sora: NOW we can ask?

Goofy: It's not like we can use that big old door anymore. It's completely 
gone.

Sora: Yeah, we closed it after beating Ansem.

Jiminy: And we certainly can't ask the King or Riku.

Sora: 'Cause you wouldn't LET me ask.

(Dale pushes Chip out of the way)

Dale: Only King Mickey can open a door to the realm of darkness.

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Huh?

(Chip pushes Dale away and Jiminy hops down)

Chip: It's because he has a special Keyblade of darkness. He figured out 
how to make it open the way.

Sora (sighing): Oh...

Goofy: Gawrsh, what'll we do then?

(Donald groans)

Sora: May my heart be our guiding key. It'll show us the way.

(Sora stands and summons the Keyblade, aiming it ahead of him. The tip

Jiminy, Donald & Goofy: A gate!

(Sora puts away the Keyblade)

Sora: But where does it lead?

Donald: It doesn't matter! Go!

Goofy: Hurry, Sora!

Sora: Okay.

(Sora sits at the controls and pilots the ship through the wormhole, the 
portal closing behind them with a ripple. The bright warm sun shines down 
on the sandy beaches of the Destiny Islands. Sora, Donald and Goofy walk 
along the seashore)

Sora: Why do you think that gate took us here?

(Walking further down the beach, Sora comes upon a Keyblade in the sand, 
the teeth of the blade forming the shape of an 'E'. Sora kneels down and 
picks it up)

Sora: A Keyblade?

Donald: It looks so old.

(He holds it in both hands, looking it over)

Sora: How did it end up here?

Goofy: Hmm, maybe it's another guiding key.

Sora: Sure, but to guide us where?

(He aims it forward and a beam erupts from the blade, striking a corner of 
the beach where a tree meets a rockface. The area glows, revealing a door. 
They rush over to it)

Goofy: A door!

Donald: Let's go.

(Sora closes his eyes, steeling himself)

Sora: Not you guys.

Donald & Goofy: Huh?

(Sora takes a few steps forward)

Sora: The realm of darkness--it isn't safe for you.

Donald: Forget it. I'm going.

Goofy: Yeah. You can't make a whole pint without us.

Sora: Come on, guys, think about it. Even the King and Riku struggled in the 
realm of darkness. Someone needs to stay out here, just in case. If 
something happens to the rest of us, you two need to carry on.

Donald (sadly): Sora... (angrily) Stop it!

Goofy: We understand, but we don't want you goin' someplace dangerous on 
your own.

Sora: Thanks, guys. But I'll be fine. I'll make sure Riku and the King are 
safe. Trust me.

(He smiles and Donald and Goofy exchange concerned looks. They nod softly 
to each other)

Donald: You promise to be good?

Goofy: And come home nice and safe?

Sora: Right.

(Sora turns around and enters the Secret Place. In the Dark World...)

Mickey: Riku, look!

(The Demon Tower wriggles in the air, bending over and twisting into Riku, 
knocking the Keyblade from his arms. It dissipates when it hits the sand)

Mickey (gasping): Riku!

(The swarm of Heartless knocks Mickey off his feet and he also drops his 
Keyblade, consumed by the swarm. Riku lifts himself up)

Riku: Mickey!

(The Demon Tower coalesces under swirling winds into an orb of darkness 
before Riku's very eyes. Purple fragments gather within the orb, pushing 
out of it. The bubble bursts and a dark figure leaps out landing on the 
gray sand. King Mickey watches from his prison in the orb as the dark figure 
walks toward his Keyblade, picking it up)

????: This Keyblade...

(Mickey gasps at the familiar voice)

Mickey: Is it her?

(The darkness peels away at the woman, revealing blue hair)

????: Mickey...

(She turns, revealing her yellow eyes)

Anti-Aqua: You're too late.

Riku: Aqua?

Mickey: What happened?

Anti-Aqua: You abandoned me, that's what. Left me in this shadow prison 
for more than a decade, knowing what it would do to me...

Mickey: I'm sorry. It's all my fault.

(She turns and walks to the shoreline)

Anti-Aqua: I reached this shore after endless wandering. Waited forever for 
help to arrive. But no one ever came.

(She walks over the water)

Anti-Aqua: I lost my Keyblade. Had no means of fighting my way back through 
the Heartless. You should have known I was stranded. Do you have any idea 
how lonely it is here?

(These words speak to Riku)

Anti-Aqua: How frightening it is to have no one?

(Riku clenches his fist in the sand)

Anti-Aqua: All that's left in my heart is misery and despair...and now, you 
can share it!

(Riku walks toward her)

Riku: There's no need. Got my own.

(In Riku's heart, a version of Riku from the past wearing the dark clothes 
of his possessed self walks to his side, the Riku Replica. In his hand he 
holds a special Keyblade, the Way to the Dawn. He looks over at Riku and 
smirks, before vanishing into particles of light. Riku clenches his fist 
again and summons his Keyblade, walking over the water after Aqua. The orb 
holding Mickey floats over the water between them, becoming a swirling mass 
of Shadow Heartless once more. He strikes at the swirling mass, sending 
Shadows flying left and right. The Demon Tower takes on a purple aura and 
splashes downward, the Heartless's eyes glowing red, as Anti-Aqua appears, 
raising the Keyblade in her hands)

Anti-Aqua: Enough!

(She summons large icy spikes, sending them careening toward Riku, before 
releasing the Demon Tower once again. Riku lands back on the water, 
breathing heavily)

Riku: Sora...

(A light shines from above and a door appears, the same door from the 
Destiny Islands. Sora soars in, landing with a splash on the water)

Sora (smiling): I made it!

(Riku smiles back at Sora and dispels his Keyblade as the Demon Tower 
swirls in front of them. Both Sora and Riku hold their arms out together, 
eminating a brilliant white light. Above, two colorful Keyblades, 
Nightmare's End and Mirage Split join together to form a giant two-handled 
blade. Sora and Riku lift their arms, raising the powerful Keyblade, which 
glows with a warm light. They throw their arms forward and the light washes 
over the Demon Tower, dispersing the Shadows inside. They release Mickey 
from their hold, sending him falling to the beach with a shout. Riku rushes 
over to him and Anti-Aqua races after him. She raises the Keyblade as Riku 
summons his just in time. The blades clash, sending up a gigantic splash. As 
the misting water falls away, Sora is holding back Aqua's Keyblade from 
Riku, sparks flying from the blades' contact. Riku stands with his mouth 
agape. Anti-Aqua leaps backward. Sora looks back at Riku, giving him a 
reassuring smile, which Riku returns)

Riku: How, Sora?

(Sora dispels his Keyblade and summons the one he found on the island)

Sora: I...had a little help. Watch over the King. I've got this.

Riku: Okay.

(Riku rushes back to Mickey as Sora dispels the Master's Defender in favor 
of his own Keyblade to face down Anti-Aqua. She teleports over the water, 
sending a strike of dark energy in his direction. She spirals on the water, 
summoning a dark Blizzard spell. Two identical clones appear wielding the 
same spell, closing in on Sora. They release shards of ice that whiz by 
Sora's head, just missing him, before encircling him in a glowing snowflake. 
He narrowly dodges, but is struck by an icicle. He runs forward, but Anti-
Aqua teleports three times in succession, causing him to miss with each 
strike. For a moment, he sees no one on the water, waiting with bated 
breath, but then he turns his head. She walks slowly away from him)

Anti-Aqua: Shouldn't have abandoned me...

(Sora's eyes lock onto her and he leaps into the air. Suddenly, she 
cartwheels to the side and strikes again. Sora catches himself, but at his 
chance to strike, she vanishes again. She reappears with multiple illusory 
copies of herself)

Anti-Aqua: I've wandered the shadows endlessly...

Anti-Aqua: You don't know what true loneliness is...

Anti-Aqua: I've waited for so long...

Anti-Aqua: Now you can share in the terror I've felt!

(Sora sends multiple projectile attacks until they hit their mark, exposing 
the true Anti-Aqua as the doppelgängers disappear. As Anti-Aqua reels back 
from the onslaught, Sora goes in for the final blow. She takes a few steps 
back, holding her head as darkness pools at her feet. With labored breaths, 
she stumbles backwards, releasing her hold on the Star Cluster Keyblade. It 
glows and disappears away from her. As she falls backwards if in slow-
motion, the darkness she harbors chips away. Aqua lands in the pool of 
darkness and sinks into the water. Above, a light shines through the blue 
abyss. She opens her equally blue eyes)

Aqua: So...this is the end.

(She closes her eyes, assuming for the final time)

Sora: Aqua!

(At the voice, she opens them again seeing a boy holding out his hand, 
reaching for her. She met this boy once. What was his name?)

Aqua: Sora...

(She extends her hand and they touch, a brilliant light erupting from it. 
Warm like the sun. She opens her eyes. The sky is blue and the waves are 
calm and the sand is soft. In the haze of the light from the Destiny 
Islands, Aqua sees Ventus and Terra)

Ventus: Aqua!

Terra: Aqua!

(Her surprise turns to comfort)

Aqua: Ven... Terra...

(The haze starts to clear and the images of Ven and Terra become that of 
Sora and Riku)

Sora: Aqua!

Riku: Aqua!

Aqua: It's you...

Mickey: Thank goodness. You're awake!

(She turns to see him)

Aqua: Mickey...

(She looks around at the environment, still sitting on the sand)

Aqua: Are these...the Destiny Islands?

Mickey: That's right.

Aqua: When did they fall to darkness?

(Riku shakes his head with a smile)

Riku: You're in the realm of light.

(The revelation strikes a chord, the emotion welling up inside her, the 
weight of the loneliness and despair that she had been holding onto for 
years suddenly exits her body in the form of tears. Seeing this, Sora 
extends a warm hand)

Sora: You're home.

(His smile is infectious)

Donald & Goofy: You're home!

(Donald rushes forward to hug her, along with Mickey. Goofy joins in)

Mickey: Welcome home.

(Sora grabs hold of Goofy and they all release a relieving laughter. Riku 
puts a hand on Sora's shoulder)

Sora: We did it!

(Meanwhile in Radiant Garden, Vexen speaks with Demyx)

Demyx: WHAAA--?!

(Vexen clamps a hand over Demyx's open mouth)

Vexen (hissing): Quiet, you dunce!

(He looks around warily and Demyx releases his hand)

Demyx: But, dude, why would you pick me?

Vexen: I cannot let the chosen catch wind of this, understand?

Demyx: Oh, I see! It's because I got benched!

(He wags a finger in Vexen's face)

Vexen (yelling): I got "benched" too!

Demyx: Wha--

(Demyx covers Vexen's mouth this time)

Demyx: Hey! Quiet!

(Vexen looks around again and Demyx lets up. Vexen coughs awkwardly, 
regaining his composure, and sighs, turning away from Demyx)

Demyx: Okay, man, look. Real talk? Backstabbing those guys would be stupid. 
If they find out, we are yesterday's toast. I mean, what's in it for me?

Vexen: Forgiveness.

Demyx: Huh? For what?

Vexen: Men like us--in the pursuit of science, we sometimes make terrible 
mistakes. Lose sight of our mission to help people. But now I can help 
someone with my research. Now, I can atone.

(Demyx narrows his eyes)

Demyx: I'm not a scientist.

(He turns away, but Vexen rushes after him)

Vexen: Wait, wait, wait!

(He grabs him by the shoulder)

Demyx: C'mon, dude. I'm useless, I'm chicken, we're not friends. I can 
count the number of times you and I have hung out on one hand--LESS than 
one hand! I didn't even KNOW you in the old life!

Vexen: Fine, FINE! But listen.

(He waves him closer and whispers in Demyx's ear)

Demyx: Huh? No way!

Vexen: It's true. The whole thing was HIS idea.

Demyx: Huh? No stinkin' way.

Vexen: He wants to atone too. But, he is one of the chosen, so his hands 
are tied. Hence my actions on his behalf, hence my need for you to act on 
MY behalf should all go awry. As you said, we are far from friends. No one 
would ever suspect you.

Demyx: Hmm... So I'm not doing any fighting?

Vexen: Correct. And more importantly, no benchwarming.

(He smiles and does a small leap)

Demyx: Ha! Yeah baby! Sign me up.

(He swings around making happy fists in the air as Vexen rolls his eyes)

Demyx: Yes! Demyx time.

(Inside the castle, Ienzo stares at the computer screen, which displays an 
image of Ansem the Wise from a decade ago)

Ienzo: We've come a long way toward reconstructing Roxas's heart. But a 
vessel... Without that... Yeah, right. Bodies don't grow on trees, Ienzo. 
It's the backup plan or nothing now. But...the backup plan isn't a true 
solution.

(A corridor of darkness appears behind him)

?????: Finally. 'Bout time.

(Ienzo whirls around, seeing Demyx enter, carrying something wrapped in a 
white cloak. He chuckles, looking around)

Demyx: Ooh. Nice place.

Ienzo: Demyx? Is that you?!

(Demyx raises an arm)

Demyx: Hey, Zexion! Long time!

(Demyx lays the cloaked bundle on the floor and rotates his shoulder and 
stretches his neck)

Demyx: How's humanity treatin' ya? I rejoined the Nobodies, but, like...I 
just can't shake the feeling I've been sweet-talked, y'know?

(He walks up to Ienzo)

Demyx: We have sooo got to have a chat.

Ienzo: Whoa, back up. What?

Demyx: Oh! Sorry, sorry. I'm gettin' ahead of myself. I'm actually here on 
a top secret mission. Apparently I'm so off everyone's radar, that I'm just 
the guy to handle a special delivery.

(He walks back to the corridor of darkness and places his hands on his hips. 
He moves aside as if presenting something)

Demyx: Ta-daaah!

(Out of the corridor walks Ansem the Wise)

Ienzo (flummoxed): Master Ansem!

(The portal closes and Ansem the Wise stands with his hands behind his back)

Ansem the Wise: Ah, well me, little Ienzo.

(Aeleus and Dilan run into the room, equally shocked, both speechless. Ienzo 
steps forward, his feelings twisting and turning inside his stomach)

Ienzo (choking back tears): They told me you'd gone mad. That you abandoned 
us. I was just a boy, but I should have known better. I am truly, deeply 
sorry.

(Ansem places his hands on Ienzo's shoulders)

Ansem the Wise: I think what matters is that you recognize the mistake. 
Peace, Ienzo.

(Ienzo looks up at him)

Ansem the Wise: It was I who was consumed by hatred--who failed you in my 
obligations as your mentor. Forgive me.

(Aeleus comforts a remorseful Dilan and Demyx interjects with a nervous laugh)

Demyx: So, uh...are we cool to get on with things here?

(He points to the bundle on the floor)

Demyx: Got ya a present from Vexen. One was all he could manage for the 
time being, but hey, he figured you guys would know what to do with it.

(They look down at the replica in the cloak)

Ienzo: A vessel!

(Later, Sora, Donald and Goofy accompany Aqua down a foggy road)

Goofy: You sure about this, Aqua?

Sora: If you want, we can take you back to Master Yen Sid's tower to rest 
with Riku and the King?

Donald: Uh-huh.

Aqua: Thank you. But...Ven's expecting me. I promised to wake him. Said I'd 
be right back, but I'm not even close. I'm in for an earful.

(She smiles to herself and the trio exchange glances as they arrive at 
Castle Oblivion. Aqua takes a deep breath with her hand over her heart. 
Donald looks from Aqua to the castle, then back to Aqua. Then the castle. 
Then Aqua. Then he starts getting impatient, tapping his finger on his arm. 
Just as he decides he's finished waiting, Goofy clamps him up, muffling his 
squawking, as Aqua summons the Master's Defender. Donald taps on Goofy's 
hand to get his attention. They watch as Aqua aims the Keyblade at the 
castle doors, a Keyhole appearing with a dazzling light. Donald breaks free 
from Goofy's grip and the three stare in amazement. The wind whips around 
them and Aqua steels her resolve. She thrusts the Keyblade forward and a 
beam of light sparks forward into the Keyhole. The trio shield themselves 
from a burst of wind, while Aqua stares unblinking as the seal on the 
castle breaks. A projection of her former home rises on the face of the 
castle and the many towers and floors readjust themselves to match the 
projection, untwisting and untangling the endless halls, everything clicking 
into place. The shadowy darkness of the clouds around the castle are pushed 
back to reveal the brightest blue sky of the world knows as The Land of 
Departure. They walk forward in awe of their surroundings. Inside the 
castle, they walk through the entrance hall taking in its splendor. Aqua 
turns to face them)

Aqua: Ready?

(The three of them nod and they walk through the golden halls and ascend 
the stairs to the Great Hall, where they find Ventus sleeping in the center 
of three large chairs. Aqua rushes to his side)

Aqua: Ven.

(She touches his face and places her head to his)

Aqua: I'm sorry it took so long.

(He doesn't stir and she tries to shake him)

Aqua: Ven, wake up. Open your eyes, please!

(He still doesn't stir)

Aqua: Why? Your heart never found its way home?

???????: That was a neat trick.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy turn to see Vanitas walk in)

Vanitas: No wonder no one could find him.

Sora: Vanitas!

(Aqua rushes forward, glaring)

Aqua: Why are you here?

Vanitas: Oh, I'm sorry to interrupt your touching reunion, but surely you 
won't begrudge me a moment with my brother?

(Sora, Donald and Goofy summon their weapons and rush at him. Vanitas

before Sora can react, he disappears again. Aqua searches the room for him, 
but he reappears on top of Ven's chair)

Aqua: What?!

Vanitas: So Venty-Wenty wants to keep sleeping. What am I ever going to do 
with you?

(Aqua summons her Keyblade)

Aqua: Shut up!

(She leaps up at him, pulling back the Keyblade for a great swing. She

Vanitas: You better settle down there, "Master."

(She jumps away from him, flipping backwards to land on her feet, as he 
persues her to the floor)

Sora: Aqua, I'll handle him!

Aqua: No. I'M ending this.

Sora: But...you haven't recovered yet.

Aqua: Sorry, but you've seen me too weak, too often. Now it's my turn to 
shine.

(She created a hexagonal barrier around herself and Vanitas. The trio move 
backwards as it expands. Sora places a hand while Goofy bangs his fist on 
the barrier)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Aqua!

(Vanitas readies to fight. Demonstrating years of honing her craft, Aqua 
fights circles around Vanitas. All of the darkness he can muster fails to 
snuff out her light. In midair, she swings her Keyblade forward knocking 
him away, both fighters falling to the floor. Vanitas turns his head toward 
Ventus and cackles. He brings his Keyblade back behind his head, igniting 
the teeth of the blade and sending a meteor straight toward Ventus, creating 
a deep crack in the magical barrier. Sensing his plan, Aqua leaps to guard 
the weak point just as Vanitas sends a second meteor to finish the job. 
Aqua slams to the ground, her Keyblade vanishing, as Vanitas releases a dark 
laugh. Sora watches, helpless, as Vanitas walks over to Aqua and raises his 
blade)

Sora: Aqua!

(Sora feels a sudden tug in his chest. Above the stained glass in Sora's 
heart, Ventus floats, his eyes closed in sleep)

Ventus: I...have to wake up...

Sora: Yes. Tell me what to do.

Ventus: The power of waking...

Sora: I can't. I still don't have it yet.

Ventus: You never lost it... It sleeps...until someone needs it... Call to 
it...

Sora: I am calling...with all my heart.

(The stained glass platform shines with a light and Sora appears. He lifts 
his Keyblade and the tip glows. A Keyhole appears on the floor in front of 
him and light ripples through the stained glass. Sora rises off the platform 
and the Keyhole shines brilliantly. Soon, thousands of white birds take off 
from the Keyhole, the light growing along the glass, revealing Ventus's 
platform. Sora aims his Keyblade, shooting a beam of light at Ventus's heart)

Ventus: Thank you for always keeping me safe, Sora...

(Ventus's eyes begin to open as Sora watches Ven's heart ascend, finally 
released. The light shining from Ven's body catches Vanitas's attention as

Ventus: Aqua!

(He strikes Vanitas's blade, clenching his teeth, and the clash between 
light and darkness spills over, shattering the barrier. It settles around

bites his tongue and leaps over them silently)

Vanitas: Three guardians is more than I care to face. But now that my 
brother is awake...I'm just certain that he'll come to visit.

(He disappears in a corridor of darkness and the group dispels their 
weapons. Ven helps Aqua stand)

Sora: Aqua, are you all right?

Aqua: Yes. I'm fine, Sora.

(Ventus pauses momentarily, noting the similarity between Sora and Vanitas)

Ventus: Huh?! You're...Sora?

Sora: Yup. Hey, Ventus.

(He extends a hand)

Ventus: I get it. You were my second chance.

Sora: Huh?

(Ventus smiles, shaking the thought away, and takes Sora's hand)

Ventus: Call me Ven.

(Aqua touches his head)

Aqua: Good morning, Ven.

Ventus: Good morning, Aqua.

(Later, the seven guardians of light, along with Donald and Goofy meet in

Ventus: Thank you.

Aqua: No, just the opposite.

Aqua: That's wonderful.

Aqua: Good for you!

(Mickey blushes)

Sora: Yeah, rub it in...

(They all laugh)

Aqua: Sora, you probably don't remember...

(He gives her a sheepish smile)

Aqua: Kairi?

(Axel clears his throat again, more forcefully this time)

Ventus: Sorry, Lea.

Goofy: He's always prepared.

Ventus: Let's share stories when Terra's back.

Aqua: Yeah.

(Meanwhile in Twilight Town, Maleficent walks through the Tram Common. She

Maleficent: I agree. Our search ends today.

Maleficent: You cannot find the unfindable. The box does not exist.

(She taps her staff against the ground)

Maleficent: Silence, imbecile. I mean the box does not exist NOW.

Pete: Is that some kinda riddle? Just where we s'posed to be lookin'?

Maleficent: Light and darkness are fated to clash. A Keyblade War is upon

Pete: That's it?! But when's MY big moment?

Maleficent: You will have it soon enough. Once I possess the box, our real 
work can begin.

(She enters a corridor of darkness and Pete, groaning, follows her in. 
Elsewhere in Twilight Town, Axel sits atop the clock tower with three bars 
of sea-salt ice cream. He bites into one with a sad look on his face)

Axel: Well, Roxas... I shoulda been there for you by now, but here we are.

????: Shouldn't you say good-bye to your REAL home?

(He looks up, stunned, as Saïx enters from around the corner)

Axel: Why...

Saïx: I'm not here to fight. Relax.

Saïx: ...and two for good luck?

(Saïx begins to eat his ice cream)

Saïx: Got it memorized? Back when we were still friends, we used to sneak 
into the castle. 

Axel: Yeah...

Saïx: And we made a friend there, a girl. We apprenticed to Ansem the Wise 
to rescue her.

(These words sting Axel)

Axel: I did not give up. One day we're apprentices, the next Ansem the Wise

Saïx: Following Xehanort's Nobody was the only way to discover what

Axel: So? You found her? I helped you rise up the ranks, so I hope it paid

Saïx: I'm afraid not. Nary a trace. I started to wonder if we'd imagined

Axel: Well, then, you blew it! Wise up already and just quit.

Saïx: Face it. Roxas is just like our other friend.

Saïx: Gone forever. You need to accept that.

Axel: Yeah. Don't need 'em.

(Saïx smirks)

Saïx: I expect no less.

(He disappears in a corridor of darkness and Axel's face softens in the

????: How long have you known that I was with you?

Riku: You took that as a sign?

Riku Replica: Maybe. I'd rather face my end with you than in darkness.

Riku Replica: Yeah. But I'm not done yet. Got one last thing to see through.

(Sora and Kairi sit on the small island next to the Seashore, watching Riku)

Kairi: Here.

Sora (surprised): Huh?

(He looks down at the paopu fruit and up to Kairi's smiling face)

Kairi: Tomorrow's fight will be our toughest yet. I want to be a part of

(He takes the fruit from her)

Sora: Kairi, I'll keep you safe.

(Kairi shakes her head)

Kairi: Let ME keep YOU safe.

(What once was just a symbol drawn on a cave wall has now become real. They 
stare into each other's eyes in the glow of the setting sun. The next day,

Mickey: It's time. The Keyblade Graveyard is up ahead.

(Aqua, Ven, Donald and Goofy nod)

Sora: Someone's coming.

(Up ahead, through the hazy air, Master Xehanort walks toward them, a dark 
glint in his eye. He bares his teeth)

Master Xehanort: Legend has it that darkness once covered the world. We know 
so little about the Keyblade War--only that it was just the beginning. If 
ruin brings about creation, what, then, would another Keyblade War bring? 
When the darkness falls, will we be found worthy of the precious light the 
legend speaks of?

(Ansem, Seeker of Darkness appears to his right)

Ansem: Or will all of creation be instead returned to the shadows? Today, we 
will recreate the legend and see.

(Xemnas appears to Xehanort's left)

Xemnas: But first... Your light shines far too brightly. It must be

(Vanitas and Young Xehanort appear in front of them)

Vanitas: Only when your hopes have been broken by battle upon battle can the

Young Xehanort: And break you is what we shall do. It has been etched.

(Darkness eminates from the five of them and consumes the landscape.

Sora: Look at how many there are!

(Donald, Goofy, Kairi and Axel show faces of concern and Mickey summons

Mickey: Okay, gang. Get ready!

Goofy: Everybody else has gone on ahead.

Donald: We gotta move!

(They walk through a long crevice, catching up to the others at the edge

Mickey: Is everybody okay?

(Axel gives a thumbs-up)

Sora: C'mon, let's go.

(Aqua and Ven nod before something up ahead catches Ven's attention. As

Ventus: Terra!

(Ventus runs toward him)

Aqua: Ven!

(Ven grabs Terra's wrist)

Ventus (joyfully): Terra! We found you!

(Aqua catches up and looks into Terra's eyes)

Aqua: Terra, please say you're in there.

(Terra's eyes move only slightly and Aqua pulls Ven away from him as the

Ventus: What gives, Aqua?

Aqua: I know that you're not him.

(Ven eyes grow wide)

Aqua: Now, let our friend go!

(Terra smiles and closes his eyes. They watch as his hair turns white,

Mickey: He IS their thirteenth.

(He brims with the power of darkness)

Terra-Xehanort: Today is the day you all lose.

Aqua: What?!

Terra-Xehanort: Before you even face the thirteen, every last one of you

(He summons his Keyblade)

Terra-Xehanort: The Chi-blade will still be forged.

Sora: We're not gonna lose to you.

(Xehanort moves quick as lightning, while Aqua paralyzes, and strikes Ven

Aqua: Ven!

Sora: That's it!

(Sora summons his Keyblade and runs to strike Xehanort, but the man stops 
his Keyblade just inches from his hand with a Gravity spell. Try as he 
might, Sora can't move the blade in any direction. Xehanort widens his 
fingers, knocking Sora away. He turns his attention to Kairi, but Axel moves 
to cover her, and Xehanort knocks him through a boulder)

Kairi: Axel!

(Xehanort raises his blade and Sora gets up, rushing toward her)

Mickey: No! Sora!

(Donald and Goofy run after him as Sora grabs hold of Kairi, covering her. 
Xehanort brings his blade down, slamming into Goofy's protective shield. 
They both go flying in opposite directions. Donald focuses and a magic 
circle appears underneath him. King Mickey's mouth drops and Goofy lands on 
the ground)

Goofy: Donald, don't!

Donald: Zettaflare!

(An incredibly powerful burst of energy explodes from Donald's magic wand, 
enveloping Xehanort and casting him away. Sora smiles once the flare dies 
down, but the wand falls from Donald's hand and he collapses to the ground. 
Sora stands frozen as Mickey, Goofy, Kairi, Riku, and Aqua run over to 
their fallen companions)

Aqua: Ven...

(Sora is stunned)

Sora: This can't be real.

(A dark pool emerges from the ground, frothing with malice, as the Demon

Riku: Pull it together, Sora! We haven't lost them. They still have their 
hearts. But we have to protect them.

Sora: Right!

(Aqua walks up to them as the swirling mass of Heartless grows more violent)

Aqua: We stand together.

(Sora and Riku nod. The three run forward and summon their Keyblades. Aqua

Aqua: Mickey, Kairi, Goofy, watch the others.

Mickey: No, we should all get to safety, while we still can.

Riku: It's too late for that.

(From different corners of the Graveyard, more Demon Tides arrive and merge

faced before. From within, Aqua sees something that terrifies her)

Aqua: It can't be... No...

(She lowers her Keyblade as the despair settles in and before anyone can 
react, the Demon Tide strikes her down)

Riku: Aqua!

(The squirming evil sweeps along the ground, carrying Ventus, Kairi and

is pulled back into the raging cyclone by the Demon Tide. Sora drops the 
Keyblade, falling to his knees, and screams at the top of his lungs, 
overcome with grief as Riku rushes to his side)

Riku: Sora!

Sora: They're gone. Kairi, Donald... Goofy, the King... Gone forever.

(Tears well up in his eyes)

Sora: What do we do?

(Riku is at a loss for words)

Sora: Without them...I... All my strength came from them. They gave me all 
of it. Alone, I'm worthless.

(His tears fall to the ground)

Sora: We've lost... It's over.

(As Sora cries, Riku resists the urge to let him continue. He clenches his 
fist and stands up)

Riku: Sora, you don't believe that. I know you don't.

(Riku walks forward as the Demon Tide swirls closer. He plants his foot on 
the ground and raises his Keyblade, shielding Sora. As the Tide approaches, 
he slams his blade into the swarm, the force of the wind blowing through 
their clothes. He rages against the force of the Tide, his body blackening 
as Sora watches. Even with all of his strength, the Heartless overtake him 
and proceed to wash over Sora. And so, as foretold, darkness prevailed, and 
light expired...)

Boy in Black: Checkmate.

(The Boy in White scans the chessboard)

Boy in Black (smiling): And so darkness prevails, and light expires. You 
need a new strategy.

Boy in White: My move, isn't it?

(The Boy in Black scans the board and the Boy in White lifts his final white 
piece)

Boy in Black: Huh?

(The Boy in White places it on the far edge of the board)

Boy in White: It's not over.

Boy in Black: C'mon. That's not fair. I know I had you.

Boy in White: Yes, you nearly did. But, a game's no fun if you know where 
it's going. There's more to light than meets the eye. I told you.

(Behind the single white piece carrying a crown token, seven more white 
pieces appear on the board and the boy smiles)

Boy in White: Some light comes from the past.

(On an endless sea and sky stretching onward to infinity, a light shines 
onto the transparent body of Sora. Sora opens his eyes and sits up, taking 
stock of the world he finds himself in. He stands, the water splashing 
beneath his feet paired with no other sound at all)

Sora: Where am I?

(He wanders the bright expanse, searching for answers)

????????: Can't stay away, now, can you?

(He looks around for the source of the voice)

Sora: Hello?

(A tiny light sparkles down in front of him, making an odd mewling sound, 
it reaches down to the water, which ripples as if something had set its 
feet down on it. There is a bright flash, causing Sora to shield his eyes 
as a small cat wearing a cape and a coin purse appears in front of him)

????????: The name's Chirithy. And this is The Final World.

Sora: I'm Sora. What's the..."Final World"?

Chirithy: There's nothing else beyond this. You've wandered here more than 
once before on your visits to the Station of Awakening, buuut...I let that 
slide. The edges of sleep and death touch, and one can't help the occasional 
crossover.

Sora: Wait, "death"?

Chirithy: Yes. The natural end for those whose hearts and bodies perish 
together. But some persist, and arrive here.

Sora: My heart and body perished? Um, does that mean...

Chirithy: Something is holding you here--refusing to let you go. You're 
hanging by a thread.

Sora: What about my friends?

Chirithy: I'm afraid that no one else arrived with you. And if they're not 
here, they're either gone forever, or they're clinging to the world you 
came from.

Sora: I'm going back!

(He summons his Keyblade and starts to leave in a rush)

Chirithy: Whoa, whoa! How exactly?

(He turns back)

Chirithy: You can't just wander out like your other visits.

Sora: What?

Chirithy: I told you. The other times you came here by your own choice. This 
time is very different. To become your old self again and return to the 
real world, you'll have to piece yourself back together in this world first.

Sora: Agh! Why am I in pieces?!

Chirithy: What? No, not literally, of course. You're conceptually in pieces. 
On the inside, who knows, but on the outside you're just fine.

(Sora dispels the Keyblade)

Sora: Oh, okay. You kinda freaked me out there!

(He puts his hands behind his head casually)

Chirithy: Oh boy...

(Chirithy shakes it off)

Chirithy: Usually, only a heart can reach The Final World. But since you've 
clearly managed to retain some kind of form, that can only mean your body 
was cast into this world as well.

Sora: Okay, so...then if I can find my body, that means I'll be able to go 
back?

Chirithy: Precisely. But there's a lot of you to find. You're going to be 
busy.

(Chirithy vanishes in a burst of light and Phantom Soras appear, wandering 
around the endless expanse)

Sora: These must be pieces of me.

(Once Sora has collected the wandering Phantom Soras, a portal appears and 
the top of his body has begun fading in again. He sees a strange glimmer 
in the midst of the never-ending sky and approaches it. It sparkles fading 
in and out in the shape of a star)

Sora: Hello?

Star: Good day.

Sora: Oh cool! You can talk.

Star: You look like a person. How is it that you retain your appearance? 
Are you special?

(Sora looks himself over, unsure what to say)

Sora: Umm... I'm a little hazy on the details.

Star: As are we all.

Sora: So whose heart are you?

Star: No one's anymore. They took away my name--everything about me.

Sora: No way. They couldn't have taken away your heart.

Star: Only because it pines for another.

Sora: Yeah? Someone's coming for you?

Star: I cannot be certain. He's been changed beyond recognition--his heart 
replaced with another's. But, were he to regain his old self again, he would 
be distressed by my absence. So I choose to wait here, where he can find me.

Sora: Good. You have to believe.

Star: Believe? Oh, you mean know in my heart he will return? Without any 
proof?

Sora: Exactly, BELIEVE. I thought it was all over for me, but a friend of 
mine looked me in the eye and said, "You don't believe that."

(She gives a tender laugh and Sora smiles)

Sora: So, uh...who did this to you? Heartless steal hearts, so...a Nobody?

Star: A...somebody.

Sora: Really? Hmm... Well, I wish I could help...but my situation's no better.

(He sits down, his eyes to the sky)

Star: You must see to the tasks before you first.

Sora: The tasks before me? (chuckles) There's so many.

Star: All the more reason for you to make an effort.

Sora: Yeah. You're right. I just wish I knew what to do.

Star: Here you are on the brink, and yet you hold on to who you are. You 
possess a strong sense of purpose. And in that purpose you will find 
direction.

Sora (smiling): Thank you. I'm really glad we met. You cheer me up. I 
hope that friend of yours finds you soon.

Star: Thank you. Me too.

Sora: Oh, hey. If I see him, I'll tell him that you're here. What's his name?

(The Star whispers into Sora's ear and surprise shows on his face)

Sora: Huh?

Star: Our secret.

(He looks around before standing up again. Soon after, Sora finds more 
glittering stars floating in the abyss, each telling a different story)

Star 2: I found myself here, lighter than before. Unburdened. All my pain 
and responsibility, gone. But something in this new ease keeps catching 
at the corners of my mind. Is it all right for me to be here like this? 
There is a faint memory. A sound. Others may have found it grating, but it 
warmed my heart. That crying... I have to find it. Embrace it. The sweet 
weight I carried. My dear, beloved burden.

Star 3: Whoever said love and hate are two sides of the same coin is a liar. 
The second our eyes would meet, we were at each others' throats, every 
time. The idea of us as friends is laughable. I'm finally my own here, and 
what a relief! Just...not as big a relief as I'd thought. It's weird. 
Something's just...missing. Ugh, is that how this works? Did I keep going 
back for another fight just so we could spend the time together? Maybe it's 
not as simple as "like" or "hate." The heart's a complex thing. Wonder if 
he feels this lonely, too... Takes two to have a fight, after all.

Star 4: We were always together. Practically joined at the hip. We'd wear 
the same clothes, eat the same food, go the same places. We were an 
identical pair--like walking alongside a mirror. So why is it just me here 
now? There's this...this feeling. Calling to me. Pulling at me. And now I 
share it. Feel it as my own. We are always together.

Star 5: "I have nothing left to teach you." I had thought those words would 
make him happy, but it was sorrow that clouded his face. I had shared all I 
know, my every technique. What more did he seek from me? I never heard the 
answer. Time passed on, and...here we are. But now, since we've parted, I 
think I understand. He wanted the same thing I did. This wasn't just about 
passing on knowledge. It was a communion. A connecting of hearts.

Star 6: I kept telling everyone we were just friends, but he crept into my 
head. Into my heart. It started to feel weird being together. I stepped 
back, and he never stepped in to close the distance. I wonder how he saw 
it. Wonder how he feels. ...What's this emotion, filling me? It's over-
powering. It's him. I have to respond. I have to tell him how I really feel.

Star 7: Did I matter? What I ever there at all? I thought I'd found my 
place, surrounded by people I trusted. But look there. I'm gone, yet they 
go on meeting up just the same. Hm? The table's set wrong. There are too 
many glasses... Oh. Added a new member, have they? That didn't take long. 
That was my seat. That was MY place at the table. Their glasses clink 
against the newcomer's, one after the next. No, this is not my place. Maybe 
it never was.

Star 8: We spent so many years together. A lifetime. It wasn't all sunshine 
and rainbows, of course. We had our share of troubles. Sorrows, too. But 
all of it is dear to me now, every minute we had. We got to experience so 
much. I have no regrets. At least, that's what I thought. Special occasions 
may stand out, but there's nothing so precious as the quiet days between 
them. That's what a life is, really...

Star 9: I was defeated. That was supposed to be it. I'd just...fade away. 
Yet a part of me remains. But why? I have no regrets. No reason to cling to 
this life. I turn these questions over in my head again and again, and 
again and again I remember. Our clash. The feeling of exhilaration. Of 
pleasure. I can see his face clearly in my mind. He wore the same grin as 
mine. I would dearly love to cross blades with him again...

Star 10: After long years of service, my one regret is that I must pass on 
before my master. I suspect he will not notice my absense. I doubt he so 
much as knew my name. Yet how, then, can I explain this sight? The artworks 
that I was tasked with tending now bear a thin layer of dust. It seems he 
expressly commanded that none of the remaining staff take up my work. What 
can that mean, save that he saw me not as one among many, but as an 
individual? That he feels my absence. Grieves for me. I am awash with 
gratitude at the thought of it. I must do all that I can to reciprocate...

Star 11: Oh, good. If you're speaking to me, I suppose I must exist. I feel 
a consciousness, or memories, perhaps. Feelings. They pass through my mind 
one after the next, but none of it feels real. And that was fine. I'd 
resigned myself to simple forget. To let it all slip away. But there was 
one piece I couldn't let go of--a fragment I couldn't forget. Maybe that 
sliver of memory is what's kept me here this whole time...

Star 12: That's strange. I'm running and running, but I can't get to Papa. 
Oh! This is hide-and-seek! I love hide-and-seek! I"m going to find Papa. 
He'll be so proud. Hmm... I can't find him. I give up, Papa! Come out! Come 
out! ...I've looked so hard for him. Isn't he looking for me? Wait, that's 
Papa's voice. I hear his voice! It's that light! I understand, now. I just 
have to run toward that light!

Star 13: Sora?

Sora: Yes?

Star 13: It's me, Naminé.

Sora: Naminé?

Naminé: I'm so glad that you managed to hold on to who you are.

Sora: Why are you here?

Naminé: I was in Kairi's heart, but then we were struck by a powerful 
darkness...and I woke up here.

Sora: And Kairi?

Naminé: I can feel her heart. She's fighting with all her strength to keep 
you from fading away.

Sora: So, the reason I retained my form in this place...

Naminé: It's because she's holding you together. Go to her.

Sora: I'm trying. But, what about you? I can't just leave you stuck here.

Naminé: It's okay. Really. Kairi is where I came from. So, once she's safe 
again, Kairi is where I'll return.

Sora: Naminé, I know that I'm supposed to thank you. The datascape doesn't 
count. I need to say the words myself. But...not like this. You and Roxas 
can't tell me you're okay with this. I know how much you're hurting. I...
felt that pain through Roxas.

Naminé: He's the one they all miss. It's...not me.

Sora: Wrong. What about me, Kairi, Donald, Goofy? The King! Roxas too, he 
misses you! And someone else special I know won't let you down.

(Even without a form, Naminé smiles)

Naminé: Sora. Thank you.

Sora: Well, then I'm gonna go save Kairi so at least you'll be free of this 
place. Okay?

(He turns)

Naminé: Oh, wait!

Sora: Huh?

Naminé: While sifting through memories, I spoke to Terra, the Keyblade 
Wielder you've been looking for. He has a strong will, and it keeps him 
tethered to the realm of light. I'll try tracing that connection. Maybe 
that'll be enough to tip the scales in the other direction.

Sora: Huh?

Naminé: Umm... Let's just say I've got your back?

Sora: That part of you--it reminds me of Kairi. Thanks, Naminé. (realizing) 
Oh! That's not the official thank-you!

(She gives a small laugh)

Naminé: Uh-huh.

Sora: Well, see ya!

(He leaves)

Naminé: Be careful.

(Sora enters the portal, ending up on a labyrinth of crystalline stone. As 
his foot touches a cube in the ground, the ground shakes and he almost 
loses his balance. Sora nervously runs forward reaching a second cube, 
which causes pillars to rise around and below him. He sees more Phantom 
Soras running, walking, dancing, jumping, swimming all around the crystal 
structure, defying the natural laws of gravity)

Sora: What a weird place.

(Sora rides a rail of light over to another pillar and strikes at a floating 
cube, causing the crystal structure to shift)

Sora: What's going on?!

(The platform rotates underneath Sora, granting him access to more of the 
structure)

Sora: I gotta put myself back together. There's no time to waste.

(He begins gathering more pieces of himself, more of his body regaining 
its opaque form)

Sora: Almost there.

(The structure shifts suddenly, and he falls off and strangely falls toward 
the structure again, where another portal appears. He activates it, stepping 
back into the expanse of sea and sky. He looks his recollected self over 
before hearing that odd mewling sound again, signaling Chirithy's 
reappearance. The cat materializes in midair and lands on the water slightly 
off-balance)

Chirithy: I see that you found them all.

Sora: Yup!

Chirithy: Then, isn't it time that you left?

(The cat points away from him and Sora crosses his arms)

Sora: Oh, thanks.

Chirithy: What? I'm doing you a big favor here, you know. Don't push it.

Sora: Hey, Chirithy. You still look like you, right? Would you like me to 
help you find YOUR pieces?

Chirithy: Oh, I don't work like that.

Sora: So, like...you're waiting for someone to rescue you?

Chirithy: Mmm...sort of?

Sora: Well, tell me who! I'll find 'em.

(He chuckles, holding a hand to his ear)

Chirithy: Uh, no no no no, that's okay. He doesn't remember the past. 
Besides, I'm sure that he's much happier with his new friends. But I'll 
wait. He'll arrive here one day.

Sora: Okay...

(He leans down)

Sora: I'll be back to visit you.

Chirithy: What?!

Sora: You and me are friends now.

Chirithy: Really? I've missed having friends.

(Sora smiles and stands back up)

Sora: Well, see ya 'round! And thanks!

(Chirithy watches him go and is puzzled when he stops in his tracks)

Sora: Umm... Could I get a hint how to save the others?

(He turns back, smiling sheepishly)

Chirithy: Seriously? Are you a Keyblade wielder, or aren't you? Haven't 
you already learned how to restore someone's heart after it's been lost?

Sora: Restore their hearts? Is that the same thing as...the "power of 
waking"?

Chirithy: I'm not sure, but...give it a shot?

Sora: No. This'll take all my heart. Okay.

(He turns around and summons the Keyblade. He holds it in front of him and 
a Keyhole appears on the reflective water. Energy gathers at the end of the 
blade and there is a flash of light. The floor shatters, revealing a gate 
with a brilliant beam of light shining up into the sky) 

Chirithy: Look for the light in the darkness!

(Sora gives Chirithy a small smile before entering the light)

Chirithy: May your heart be your guiding key.

(Sora returns to his weakest moment)

Riku: Sora, you don't believe that. I know you don't.

(Riku walks forward as the Demon Tide swirls closer. He plants his foot on 
the ground and raises his Keyblade, shielding Sora. As the Tide approaches, 
he slams his blade into the swarm, the force of the wind blowing through 
their clothes. He rages against the force of the Tide, his body blackening 
as Sora watches. Even with all of his strength, the Heartless overtake him 
and proceed to wash over Sora. Sora floats in the abyss as streaks of light 
pass over him. He awakens, seeing the light ahead of him)

Sora: Riku!

(He reaches toward the light)

Sora: Riku! Answer me!

(The light grows brighter as he flies closer. Soaring into the light, he 
finds himself in familiar territory)

Sora: This is Herc's world. Is Riku here?

(Sora ascends the golden stairs warily)

Sora: There's nobody here.

Jiminy: Gee, I'm here!

(Jiminy Cricket pops out of Sora's hood and into his hand)

Sora: Jiminy! You're okay!

Jiminy: Well, "okay" might be a stretch, but what are we waitin' for? We 
need to find the others!

(Sora smiles down at him)

Sora: Right!

(Sora proceeds into the Courtyard, finding a transparent comatose Riku 
floating above a massive golden sacrificial tripod)

Sora: Riku!

(Sora rushes toward him and a swirling cloud of darkness appears above 
Riku. It coalesces into a Heartless holding a large staff and trailing 
chains beneath it: The Lich. It gazes down at Riku with its glowing yellow 
eyes, holding out a hand over his body. Riku's heart appears over him and 
the Lich encircles it with chains to Sora's horror. The heart vanishes and 
the Lich floats toward the Corridors. Sora pursues the Lich through the 
archway, finding a group of Shadow and Neoshadow Heartless in the way)

Jiminy: Forget the small fry! We gotta go after the one in charge.

(Sora blasts through them and races to the Cloud Ridge, more Heartless 
appearing before him)

Jiminy: We'll never stop 'em all. Leave 'em, Sora. We gotta keep going!

(The Lich flies into a dark portal and Sora follows. It takes him up to the 
Apex where the Lich waits. The Heartless shoots fireballs at Sora, but he 
dodges and pummels the Lich until Riku's heart flies out of him. The chains 
shatter and the Lich escapes through the portal once more)

Sora: Hey! Wait!

(The heart floats away into the air and Jiminy appears)

Jiminy: There's no need to worry, Sora. He'll return to the place he fell, 
like you did. We gotta focus on rescuing the others.

Sora: Okay!

(Sora and Jiminy follow the Lich through the portal. They find themselves 
floating in starlit space with six portals beneath them)

Jiminy: That scoundrel musta fled into one of those pools of shadow that're 
down below us.

Sora: Where do they lead?

Jiminy: Well, I think they might be portals to other worlds.

Sora: Okay! Maybe that's where we'll find the others.

Jiminy: If we hurry!

(Sora falls through a portal and finds himself in the Caribbean aboard a 
damaged pirate ship. The Lich chains Aqua's heart and attacks Sora with 
bullets of water. Sora dodges the attack and the Lich summons Vaporflies 
which hone in on Sora. As Sora fights the Vaporflies, the Lich creates 
images of itself. Sora strikes down a Vaporfly as one of the mirages 
explodes near him, sending him flying. He shakes it off and strikes back 
at the Lich until it gives up Aqua's heart. The heart floats away and the 
Lich escapes again)

Sora: Hold still!

(Following the Lich, Sora falls through space again)

Jiminy: We oughta search every portal the shadows control.

(Sora falls into the portal leading to Arendelle. He arrives in the Middle 
Tier of the Labyrinth of Ice where the Lich captures Goofy's heart. The 
Heartless summons multiple Winterhorns, while floating out of reach. 
Ignoring the Winterhorns, Sora locks onto the Lich, storing up projectiles 
to release, but is caught off guard when the floor buckles and he is struck 
by an ice pillar shooting up out of the floor. After returning to his feet, 
he attacks the Winterhorns only to be hit by an ice spell from the Lich, 
which freezes him momentarily. Once free, he knocks the Lich around until 
it relinquishes Goofy's heart. It retreats again into the portal)

Sora (angrily): Enough!

(Following the Heartless again, Sora finds himself in the Lobby of Monsters, 
Inc., where the Lich takes control of Donald's heart. It then releases a 
6-fold fire attack, but Sora blocks them by spinning the Keyblade. After a 
few minutes of fighting, Donald's heart is also freed and the Lich escapes)

Sora: Stop that!

(Sora follows it)

Jiminy: Let's try another portal. Aim for the ones wrapped in shadows!

(Sora falls through the portal leading to Galaxy Toys, where Ven's heart is 
taken by the Lich. The Heartless raises its arms, summoning Marionettes 
around the large central gumball machine. While Sora is focused on the 
smaller Heartless, the Lich's staff erupts with electricity. It aims several 
disc-shaped bolts of lightning at Sora, but he knocks a stuffed patchwork 
animal in the way to block most of the attack. Sora whacks the Lich with the 
Keyblade until it falls back and Ven's heart floats out of the empty heart 
in its chest, its chains falling away. The heart floats out of reach and 
the Lich returns to the portal once more)

Sora: Hey!

(Entering the portal again, Sora descends to an entrance to the Marshes in 
the Kingdom of Corona, where the Lich floats over King Mickey's body. The 
Heartless chains the mouse's heart and summons a group of Flutterings. This 
time ignoring the smaller Heartless and going straight for the Lich, Sora 
gets a few hits in before it teleports away, leaving a mirage in its wake. 
Dodging the inevitable explosion afterward, Sora rushes to the Lich, but is 
knocked back by a whirlwind that surrounds the deathly Heartless. Sora 
strikes back with a Thunder spell, sending bolts of lighting against the 
Lich, breaking the whirlwind. With the path clear, Sora strikes the Lich 
until it releases Mickey's heart and ducks back into the portal)

Sora: Hey, stop!

(Sora rushes into the portal, seeing one remaining gateway)

Jiminy: That's the last one! He must be hiding in there!

(Sora soars into the gate, landing on the streets of San Fransokyo where 
the Lich takes control of Axel's heart. The Lich sends Sora flying in the 
air with another wind spell, but he recovers only to be hit by a group of 
fireballs. Sora falls to the ground, where the Lich summons an army of 
Neoshadows. The Keyblade wielder dashes to a free-standing light pole and 
spins around it, using the momentum to leap up at the Lich. Unrelenting, he 
strikes the Lich until it stops moving, and dispels the Keyblade. The 
Heartless brims with darkness and fades away, letting go of Axel's heart. 
It floats away into the night sky. Sora walks through the city streets with 
Jiminy on his shoulder)

Jiminy: Well, Sora, I'd say we've been to every world that we can visit.

Sora: But we're one short. Where's Kairi's heart?

Jiminy: Gee, I wish I knew.

(A corridor of darkness opens in front of them and Young Xehanort walks 
through)
